  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9120a897-529e-488d-ba69-95985e3399d0'

  <span id="freeText1577393952209161426" style="display:none">Perfect for fans of "Throne of Glass" and "A Court of Thorns and Roses" by Sarah J Maas and "Daughter of Smoke and Bone" by Leigh Bardugo.<br /><br />Sworn to a goddess. One with her blade. A heart yet unbroken.<br /><br />It would have been only one more year of training. One year in the dust and wind of the Calma Desert. But Gandrett Brayton’s fate storms in disguised as a beautiful stranger with a damning secret.<br /><br />As he forces her into the service of the lord who tore her from her mother’s arms ten years ago to commit her to the Order of Vala, Gandrett is left with a choice: run, or work for the man she despises and earn the chance to see her family again. Trained with all the weapons she can wield with her hands, Gandrett must learn that at the courts of the shattered kingdom of Sives, her sword won’t help her - especially when it is her own heart on the line.<br /><br />★★★★★ “Fae, magic, and a heart-throbbing adventure will keep readers entranced until the last page.”<br /><br />Shattered Kingdom is bestselling author Angelina J. Steffort's new young adult epic fantasy romance about a girl who's heart could change the course of history.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3410133974?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ivandri Kleynhans" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ivandri Kleynhans" href="/user/show/23259071-ivandri-kleynhans">Ivandri Kleynhans</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3410133974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11552119708465393497">I was given this opportunity by the author and Bookfunnel to read this starter in a new series in exchange for an honest review. <br/><br/>To be honest, I just looked at the cover and told the author I needed to read this without even reading the synopsis. <br/><br/>This book is for anyone who loved Throne of Glass by Sarah J Maas.<br/><br/>It was a bit too quick for me. Relationships couldn't be built and one just couldn't really get a feel for the other characters.<br/><br/>Our MC, Gandrett, is a spunky warrior with unique character</span>
  <span id="freeText11552119708465393497" style="display:none">I was given this opportunity by the author and Bookfunnel to read this starter in a new series in exchange for an honest review. <br /><br />To be honest, I just looked at the cover and told the author I needed to read this without even reading the synopsis. <br /><br />This book is for anyone who loved Throne of Glass by Sarah J Maas.<br /><br />It was a bit too quick for me. Relationships couldn't be built and one just couldn't really get a feel for the other characters.<br /><br />Our MC, Gandrett, is a spunky warrior with unique characteristics. Nehelon is our typical brooding Fae male that makes you want to hate and love him at the same time. Brax and Armand first had overlapping personalities, but as Armand started to shed his arrogant prince ways, he started to bloom as a character - Brax is still a mystery which I hope to unravel in the upcoming books. As for McKenzie, I hope to read more about her too. She was a shining gem, nothing what one would have expected in such short chapters where we saw her.<br /><br />The plot twists were unexpected. I literally voiced my comments for each and every one of those to the author and she - like many awesome (evil) authors do - laughed in pure delight at the feelings that stirred within me.<br /><br />I even had the chance to pop in a few questions with the author herself to get a all-around feel of what she was thinking when she was busy putting this piece of artwork on virtual paper. Angelina is so down to earth, readily to answer questions and lay out anything that seemed confusing - she even helped me as an aspiring writer to be motivated enough and finish, not 1, but 10 chapters of my own book! <br /><br />As for the conclusion, I got tingles! It leaves a reader wondering if and what that ancient darkness could be *wink-wink*<br /><br />Overall enjoyed the book, and I am more than happy to read the next books in the series. I highly recommend this series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11552119708465393497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4145180704354841536">This book was a lot of fun. It follows our heroine Gandrett, who is enlisted to rescue a kidnapped son of a Lord. This book did an excellent job of world building and setting up pre-existing issues that caused tension among the characters. Typically, I dislike when books are compared to whatever is currently popular, but in this case it held true. I think fans of Throne of Glass would love this, as it has similarities in writing style and overall feel. <br/>I will mention that there is three potentia</span>
  <span id="freeText4145180704354841536" style="display:none">This book was a lot of fun. It follows our heroine Gandrett, who is enlisted to rescue a kidnapped son of a Lord. This book did an excellent job of world building and setting up pre-existing issues that caused tension among the characters. Typically, I dislike when books are compared to whatever is currently popular, but in this case it held true. I think fans of Throne of Glass would love this, as it has similarities in writing style and overall feel. <br />I will mention that there is three potential love interests, but there hasn't been enough relationship development thus far to reveal if these will be reciprocal (and a love triangle situation), or if this is the type of book where all men fall in love with the heroine. I didn't mind this, but I think it's worth mentioning since I know a lot of readers feel strongly about these types of tropes.<br />I am terribly picky about giving out 5-star reviews, and although I gave this 4-stars (which means a GREAT book in my opinion) I could definitely see myself giving the sequels higher ratings once there is more world building and relationship development. Overall this was a really satisfying read that tied up the overarching issues, leaving the background issues to be resolved (hopefully) in future installments. I am looking forward to reading the future sequel and can't wait to see what happens!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4145180704354841536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4546417058057389653" style="display:none">This is one of the best starts to a fantasy series I’ve read in awhile. First, it has a map! I love maps, makes me think the author has thought about the world they are building. Strong female characters that grow are also on my list of what makes a great series. Gandrett, the main character, is just that, strong, young, and smart. Nehelon, the Fae who turns her life inside out is mysterious, handsome and compelling. Steffort slowly unwinds her complex characters with humor, compassion and soul wrenching twists throughout the book. Magic, dragons and political plots supported by a beautifully written story definitely make this a must read!<br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3439197558" />
    <a title="Dawn Yacovetta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43858319-dawn-yacovetta"><img alt="Dawn Yacovetta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433986915p2/43858319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3439197558?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dawn Yacovetta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dawn Yacovetta" href="/user/show/43858319-dawn-yacovetta">Dawn Yacovetta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3439197558" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4766877477997591227">Gandrett is a strong heroine, which is something this author is becoming an expert at writing. I love the detail and colors in each scene. The adventures are magical and multi-layered, and they take us to realms in the author's mind only she can unlock. Each of the characters in this story had a particular spot in the heroine's heart, and we find, throughout the tale, where she belongs in theirs, even as they deny such things.<br/><br/>The supernatural aspect of the story adds so much depth, and we find t</span>
  <span id="freeText4766877477997591227" style="display:none">Gandrett is a strong heroine, which is something this author is becoming an expert at writing. I love the detail and colors in each scene. The adventures are magical and multi-layered, and they take us to realms in the author's mind only she can unlock. Each of the characters in this story had a particular spot in the heroine's heart, and we find, throughout the tale, where she belongs in theirs, even as they deny such things.<br /><br />The supernatural aspect of the story adds so much depth, and we find that there is more to each of the characters than we first realized. Nehelon is so much more than he lets on and shows her how to open up to the possibilities inside her. But she also finds a courage that is so much more than she knew she held within.<br /><br />The good guys are tempting, and the bad guys are despicable. The intrigue and mystery surrounding the situation makes for an exhilarating and enchanting story that moves into frightening realms and has us cheering for the heroine to succeed if only to survive. I found it impossible to put the story down and became completely engulfed in the magic of it all. I don't know where the adventure will take us next, but I look forward to finding out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4766877477997591227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3601436013" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3601436013" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1239703-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601659362p2/1239703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3601436013?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/1239703-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3601436013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8727082669991355725">Oh my oh my!<br/><br/>I am writing this review after receiving an ARC copy of the novel-- but I would have GLADLY paid real $$ for this series!<br/><br/>Steffort creates a beautiful new world for readers-- her prose and her world building are truly delightful. I was hesitant at first, since the blurb I had read made it sound similar to ACOTAR and other, rather well known fantasy. HOWEVER, the hype was worth it.<br/><br/>Gannett, our monk-like protaganist is more of a subtle character, but the interactions she has with other </span>
  <span id="freeText8727082669991355725" style="display:none">Oh my oh my!<br /><br />I am writing this review after receiving an ARC copy of the novel-- but I would have GLADLY paid real $$ for this series!<br /><br />Steffort creates a beautiful new world for readers-- her prose and her world building are truly delightful. I was hesitant at first, since the blurb I had read made it sound similar to ACOTAR and other, rather well known fantasy. HOWEVER, the hype was worth it.<br /><br />Gannett, our monk-like protaganist is more of a subtle character, but the interactions she has with other characters in the novel are the meat of the book. The beautiful writing of Steffort's book, coupled with a mysterious main character left me salivating as I read it. I ususally have a hard time putting a book down, but this was a bit of a surprise, to be honest.<br /><br />There are, I am sure, critics who will decry that the novel is full of tropes-- but they're wrong. There is a complexly woven tale here, that will certainly unfold as the series continues. I am so excited to read the next in the series-- Wicked Crown, and can't wait to see where the story takes us!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8727082669991355725" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3361561532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17932608629645300994">"Shattered Kingdom" by Angelina J. Steffort is the first book in a new epic fantasy series, featuring Gandrett Brayton, an acolyte in the Order of Vala, whose life consists of training and deprivation and, once she reaches maturity, fulfilling missions for the Order as a fighting warrior.<br/><br/>Gandrett's path takes on a brand-new nuance, as Nehelon appears at the door, intended on borrowing her skills for a covert mission: Joshua, the heir of House Brenheran, has been kidnapped by her mortal enemies, </span>
  <span id="freeText17932608629645300994" style="display:none">"Shattered Kingdom" by Angelina J. Steffort is the first book in a new epic fantasy series, featuring Gandrett Brayton, an acolyte in the Order of Vala, whose life consists of training and deprivation and, once she reaches maturity, fulfilling missions for the Order as a fighting warrior.<br /><br />Gandrett's path takes on a brand-new nuance, as Nehelon appears at the door, intended on borrowing her skills for a covert mission: Joshua, the heir of House Brenheran, has been kidnapped by her mortal enemies, the rulers of Denderlain.<br /><br />Gandrett's mission consists of infiltrate Denderlain and free Joshua, a mission that would require finesse and a whole new set of skills much different of those learn at the Order.<br /><br />Accompanied by Nehelon, who also has an agenda of his own, Gandrett embarks in a rescue mission that turns to be other than expected. Along the way Gandrett's journey turns into an epic tale of power struggle, deceit, friendship, loyalty and trust.<br /><br />Angelina J. Steffort has crafted a brand-new world, populated with fully fleshed out characters: Gandrett is a fabulous female hero, both strong and vulnerable, with a solid moral compass and a mind of her own, while Nehelon is the perfect counterpart for the quest. All secondary characters play a very important role in the story and have each a very distinct personality.<br /><br />The plot thickens page by page, revealing unforeseen twists and ramifications, that make the book into a real page-turner, and while the action maintains the reader on the edge of the seat, it is the fine humour and perfect chemistry between the characters what really makes the book exceptional. A story that lingers long after reading. I wish I could give it six stars, wait a second ..... ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ I just did!<br /></span>

<div id="review_3624199728" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3624199728" />
    <a title="Ana-Maria D.A" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/105423316-ana-maria-d-a"><img alt="Ana-Maria D.A" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603046170p2/105423316.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3624199728?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ana-Maria D.A" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ana-Maria D.A" href="/user/show/105423316-ana-maria-d-a">Ana-Maria D.A</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3624199728" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11984190367042167329">◦ I've received this book in an exchange of my honest review – NOT an ARC ◦ <br/><br/>“A miniature – Gandrett he pulverized with his magic so no one would ever learn how much her allure sang to him. And it wasn’t her face – he remebered every freckle on her cheeks, every fleck of gold in her eyes, every imperfection that made her so much more perfect – but it was her fierce heart that drew him in.”<br/><br/>Gandrett Brayton - a 17 years old girl, tore from her mother’s arms at the age of 7 and sworn to a goddess, b</span>
  <span id="freeText11984190367042167329" style="display:none">◦ I've received this book in an exchange of my honest review – NOT an ARC ◦ <br /><br />“A miniature – Gandrett he pulverized with his magic so no one would ever learn how much her allure sang to him. And it wasn’t her face – he remebered every freckle on her cheeks, every fleck of gold in her eyes, every imperfection that made her so much more perfect – but it was her fierce heart that drew him in.”<br /><br />Gandrett Brayton - a 17 years old girl, tore from her mother’s arms at the age of 7 and sworn to a goddess, becomes one with her blade. One year left before finishing her training, her fate takes a turn for the worst when a beautiful stranger appears at the priory asking specifically for Gandrett’s services. Fear creeps into her soul when she finds out the stranger is a Fae and she will have to work with him – but what she doesn’t know is that the job she has been hired to do – will require to have her own heart on the line.<br /><br />The book says its perfect for fans of “Throne of Glass” and “A court of Throns and Roses” by Sarah J. Maas and “Daughter of Smoke and Bone” by Leight Bardugo, me I’ve not read any of the books mentioned above – so I can’t say anything, however, what I can say is that I’ve found another book boyfriend and right now it feels like I’ve gathered an harem (don’t tell my boyfriend).<br /><br />On a serious note, the book has taken me into one amazing adventure. Gandrett’s story starts very heartbreaking, being a child of 7 years old and being tore from her mother arm’s to become a Child of Vala and train from such a young age, not knowing what childhood is – is sad. However, through this book you see her change from being the best fighter on the priory to save the Prince’s life, to slowly but surely falling for the fae male. You can see Gandrett’s actions are usually towards a goal and barely looses focus, to save the prince, to be able to spend time with her family – a family she hasn’t seen in 10 years, but you also see her in her worst moments, including a moment where she lost her consciousness and she wet herself. This type of things on the book really made me stop and be like WOW – she’s human. You don’t usually see moments like this on a book, is almost like normal bodily functions are taboo but not on this book. <br /><br />I’ve also loved the slow burn romance between her and the fae, her conflicted feelings regarding him, because as a Child of Vala she has made an oath to be her sole company for the rest of her days and is very intriguing when her own hear is rebelling against her own faith, making her second guess her future.<br /><br />The book has made my heart flutter with love, happiness but also fear, and the end of the book is breathtaking and ends in a cliffhanger. I’m glad the 2nd book is already out and I get the chance to read it next, because this type of suspense is going to end my life way too soon. The book is raw, full of powerful magic, the female leader is a bad-ass heroine that finishes her tasks and beyond that. The females in the book beside being godly beautiful they’re also strong, powerful and do not back down from their own tasks, even tho they might not be as strong as a male.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11984190367042167329" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3418326842" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18034331002567137862">3.5 stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I’ll need weapons,” she demanded, and he wanted to tell her that he would lay all the armament he had at her feet when the time came. If the time ever came. But now was not the time.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Characters : ⭐⭐⭐ <br/>The only one who held me captive from start to finish is Nehelon.   <span id="freeText18034331002567137862" style="display:none">3.5 stars<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’ll need weapons,” she demanded, and he wanted to tell her that he would lay all the armament he had at her feet when the time came. If the time ever came. But now was not the time.</i>
</b><br /><br />Characters : ⭐⭐⭐ <br />The only one who held me captive from start to finish is Nehelon. His narration makes me curious about what's gonna happen next, because he keeps giving us hint at the end of the chapter and then the story move on like nothing just happened. That might be what makes me finish this book. I'm curious.... Even if Gandrett (the heroine) received many attention from others characters, I feel like the romance is heading to only one person. So, it's not a reverse hareem. She keeps thinking of him when she's with anyone else. All the secondary characters too flat for me. It's their interaction maybe and not getting enough brief of the past. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Something stirred inside of him. A long-forgotten emotion that had led only to loss and pain in the past. And before she could blink her eyes open, he drew back enough to escape the draw of her quiet beauty.</b>
</i><br /><br />Plot and setting : ⭐⭐⭐⭐<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I know that many reasons why the authors using many povs is to help the plot grow better, but there's some that I want to just skip over. <br />I was just reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/52870746.Divine_Blood__Guardians_of_the_Maiden___1_" title="Divine Blood (Guardians of the Maiden, #1) by Beck Michaels" rel="nofollow noopener">Divine Blood</a> before reading this one so yeah it's hard not to compare it. Divine blood has a stronger world-building and slower plot, but this has the elements of mystery and twist that keep me going. I had no idea what the magic differences and goddess position hold in the story or why many things I think unnecessary happens, like : why does she need a carriage when she's riding horse and the carriage is even turning back in the halfway because of the roads and she doesn't need to bring anything for her mission really. That's not even a good one, the big one is how could the biological father doesn't know the lineage of his son when he's the one rising him after the mother giving him, like doesn't he know about the mother or something? The book has a fast pace from the very first chapter, so that's I'm not bored at all.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I also want to talk of the similarities to the throne of glass series in the term of the plot and characters, yes it feels similar, but the heroine in here doesn't make me rooting for her yet. She is good, but that's it. <br /><br />Well, maybe it's because this book is the first in series, so many loopholes to the series to fill. Somehow I believe that the second book going to get much better, I can see many things coming together. I'm looking forward, but no promises.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9808832839648163170">This book sparks a lot of SJM references for me which I do not hate at all! I was pleasantly surprised by the twists in the storyline and even the ending which left me with so many unanswered questions but in a pleasant way. <br/><br/>If you love SJM, a strong heroine and fantasy this will be your new favorite book. <br/><br/>Not all books are perfect unfortunately, and this one really struggled on developing relationships on paper. While I liked the characters as individuals, it was really hard to get any real con</span>
  <span id="freeText9808832839648163170" style="display:none">This book sparks a lot of SJM references for me which I do not hate at all! I was pleasantly surprised by the twists in the storyline and even the ending which left me with so many unanswered questions but in a pleasant way. <br /><br />If you love SJM, a strong heroine and fantasy this will be your new favorite book. <br /><br />Not all books are perfect unfortunately, and this one really struggled on developing relationships on paper. While I liked the characters as individuals, it was really hard to get any real connections from the pages. She was very vague about moments and conversations that really should have been put on paper, so the reader could get a sense of what the relationships were meant to look like. Everything seemed one sides. It was like Steffort drew an vague connect the dot picture for us but unfortunately didn't connect the dots leaving the reader (artist) unsure of what they were drawing. She really needed to connect those dots for us.<br /><br />I would still recommend the book and do look forward to reading the next one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9808832839648163170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mY0GYXoE99X6kkhgqy9tGR2n9GjKueW6bMnoRTI1T3WkfVKc4zt/ne6RHq4jK9Lq0p1k2BgbKNMPCVexe7KOPg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fama/j7ppQ8LQau7qOBn4NlA59S9+bD2qO5f1LVr7RFAWc4Dp9YtRx9C/XUg5NgTFnp3ZG9bfZ/LLuAg/OwsWg==')})
  }
